height="165" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Pierwsze_wy%C5%9Bcigi_w_Warszawie_%2859465%29.jpg/330px-Pierwsze_wy%C5%9Bcigi_w_Warszawie_%2859465%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Pierwsze_wy%C5%9Bcigi_w_Warszawie_%2859465%29.jpg/440px-Pierwsze_wy%C5%9Bcigi_w_Warszawie_%2859465%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3753" data-file-height="2814" /></a><figcaption>Horse Racing in <a href="/wiki/Warsaw" title="Warsaw">Warsaw</a> at <a href="/wiki/Mokot%C3%B3w_Field" title="Mokot\xc3\xb3w Field">Pole Mokotowskie</a> Race Track in 1891</figcaption></figure>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Europe">Europe</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Europe"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Olaus_Magnus_-_On_Horse_Races_on_the_Ice.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Olaus_Magnus_-_On_Horse_Races_on_the_Ice.jpg/220px-Olaus_Magnus_-_On_Horse_Races_on_the_Ice.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="102" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Olaus_Magnus_-_On_Horse_Races_on_the_Ice.jpg/330px-Olaus_Magnus_-_On_Horse_Races_on_the_Ice.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Olaus_Magnus_-_On_Horse_Races_on_the_Ice.jpg/440px-Olaus_Magnus_-_On_Horse_Races_on_the_Ice.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1300" data-file-height="600" /></a><figcaption>Horse racing in Sweden, c. 1555</figcaption></figure>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Belgium">Belgium</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Belgium"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Horse racing in Belgium takes place at three venues \xe2\x80\x93 <a href="/wiki/Hippodrome_Wellington" title="Hippodrome Wellington">Hippodrome Wellington</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ostend" title="Ostend">Ostend</a> (opened in 1883 in honour of <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Wellesley,_1st_Duke_of_Wellington" title="Arthur Wellesley, 1st Duke of Wellington">Arthur Wellesley, 1st Duke of Wellington</a>), <a href="/wiki/Hippodroom_Waregem" class="mw-redirect" title="Hippodroom Waregem">Hippodroom Waregem</a> in <a href="/wiki/Waregem" title="Waregem">Waregem</a> in Flanders and <a href="/wiki/Hippodrome_de_Wallonie" title="Hippodrome de Wallonie">Hippodrome de Wallonie</a> in <a href="/wiki/Mons,_Belgium" title="Mons, Belgium">Mons</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wallonia" title="Wallonia">Wallonia</a>.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Czech_Republic">Czech Republic</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Czech Republic"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>There are <a href="/wiki/List_of_horse_racing_venues" title="List of horse racing venues">15 racecourses</a> in the Czech Republic, most notably Pardubice Racecourse, where the country\'s most famous race, the <a href="/wiki/Velka_pardubicka" class="mw-redirect" title="Velka pardubicka">Velka Pardubicka steeplechase</a>, has been run since 1874.<sup id="cite_ref-Pardubika_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pardubika-51"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>51<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> However, the first official race was organized back in 1816 by <a href="/wiki/Francis_II,_Holy_Roman_Emperor" title="Francis II, Holy Roman Emperor">Emperor Francis II</a> near <a href="/wiki/Kladruby_nad_Labem" title="Kladruby nad Labem">Kladruby nad Labem</a>. The Czech horse racing season usually starts at the beginning of April and ends sometime in November. Racing takes place mostly at weekends and there is usually one meeting on a Saturday and one on Sunday.<sup id="cite_ref-Czech_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Czech-52"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>52<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Horse races, as well as Thoroughbred horse breeding, is organized by Jockey Club Czech Republic, founded in 1919.<sup id="cite_ref-DirTurf_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DirTurf-53"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>53<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="France">France</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: France"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_French_flat_horse_races" title="List of French flat horse races">List of French flat horse races</a>, <a href="/wiki/Category:Horse_racing_in_France" title="Category:Horse racing in France">Category:Horse racing in France</a>, and <a href="/wiki/French_flat_racing_Champion_Jockey" title="French flat racing Champion Jockey">French flat racing Champion Jockey</a></div>\n<p>France has a major horse racing industry. It is home to the famous <a href="/wiki/Prix_de_l%27Arc_de_Triomphe" title="Prix de l&#39;Arc de Triomphe">Prix de l\'Arc de Triomphe</a> held at <a href="/wiki/Longchamp_Racecourse" title="Longchamp Racecourse">Longchamp Racecourse</a>, the richest race in Europe and the third richest turf race in the world after the <a href="/wiki/Japan_Cup" title="Japan Cup">Japan Cup</a> and <a href="/wiki/The_Everest" title="The Everest">the Everest</a> with a prize of 4&#160; million Euros (approximately US$4.2&#160; million). Other major races include the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Prix_de_Paris" title="Grand Prix de Paris">Grand Prix de Paris</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Prix_du_Jockey_Club" title="Prix du Jockey Club">Prix du Jockey Club</a> (the French <a href="/wiki/Derby_(horse_race)" title="Derby (horse race)">Derby</a>) and the <a href="/wiki/Prix_de_Diane" title="Prix de Diane">Prix de Diane</a>. Besides Longchamp, France\'s other premier flat racecourses include <a href="/wiki/Chantilly_Racecourse" title="Chantilly Racecourse">Chantilly</a> and <a href="/wiki/Deauville_Racecourse" class="mw-redirect" title="Deauville Racecourse">Deauville</a>. There is also a smaller but nevertheless important jumps racing sector, with Auteil Racecourse being the best known. The sport\'s governing body is <a href="/wiki/France_Galop" title="France Galop">France Galop</a>.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Great_Britain">Great Britain</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Great Britain"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Horseracing_in_Great_Britain" class="mw-redirect" title="Horseracing in Great Britain">Horseracing in Great Britain</a></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Horseracing_in_Scotland" class="mw-redirect" title="Horseracing in Scotland">Horseracing in Scotland</a> and <a href="/wiki/Horseracing_in_Wales" class="mw-redirect" title="Horseracing in Wales">Horseracing in Wales</a></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Becher%27s_Brook,_1890.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Becher%27s_Brook%2C_1890.jpg/220px-Becher%27s_Brook%2C_1890.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="152" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/e/e7/Becher%27s_Brook%2C_1890.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="283" data-file-height="195" /></a><figcaption>1890 engraving of horses jumping the <a href="/wiki/Becher%27s_Brook" title="Becher&#39;s Brook">Becher\'s Brook</a> fence in the <a href="/wiki/Grand_National" title="Grand National">Grand National</a>. With treacherous fences combined with the distance (over 4 miles), the race has been called "the ultimate test of horse and rider".<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>54<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></figcaption></figure>\n<figure class="mw-default-size mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Eclipse(horse).jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Eclipse%28horse%29.jpg/220px-Eclipse%28horse%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Eclipse%28horse%29.jpg/330px-Eclipse%28horse%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Eclipse%28horse%29.jpg/440px-Eclipse%28horse%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="534" /></a><figcaption><a href="/wiki/Eclipse_(horse)" title="Eclipse (horse)">Eclipse</a>, an undefeated British racehorse and outstanding sire.</figcaption></figure>\n<p>Horse racing in Great Britain is predominantly thoroughbred <a href="/wiki/Flat_racing" class="mw-redirect" title="Flat racing">flat</a> and <a href="/wiki/National_Hunt_racing" title="National Hunt racing">jumps</a> racing. It was in Great Britain in the 17th to 19th centuries that many of the sport\'s rules and regulations were established. Named after <a href="/wiki/Edward_Smith-Stanley,_12th_Earl_of_Derby" title="Edward Smith-Stanley, 12th Earl of Derby">Edward Smith-Stanley, 12th Earl of Derby</a>, <a href="/wiki/Epsom_Derby" title="Epsom Derby">The Derby</a> was first run in 1780. The race serves as the middle leg of the British <a href="/wiki/Triple_Crown_of_Thoroughbred_Racing#English_Triple_Crowns" title="Triple Crown of Thoroughbred Racing">Triple Crown</a>, preceded by the <a href="/wiki/2000_Guineas_Stakes" title="2000 Guineas Stakes">2000 Guineas</a> and followed by the <a href="/wiki/St_Leger_Stakes" title="St Leger Stakes">St Leger</a>. The name "<a href="/wiki/Derby_(horse_race)" title="Derby (horse race)">Derby</a>" has since become synonymous with great races all over the world, and as such has been borrowed many times in races abroad.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>55<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Grand_National" title="Grand National">Grand National</a> is the most prominent race in <a href="/wiki/British_culture" class="mw-redirect" title="British culture">British culture</a>, watched by many people who do not normally watch or bet on horse racing at other times of the year.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>56<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Many of the sport\'s greatest jockeys, most notably Sir <a href="/wiki/Gordon_Richards_(jockey)" title="Gordon Richards (jockey)">Gordon Richards</a>, have been British. The sport is regulated by the <a href="/wiki/British_Horseracing_Authority" title="British Horseracing Authority">British Horseracing Authority</a>. The BHA\'s authority does not extend to Northern Ireland; racing in Ireland is governed on an <a href="/wiki/All-Ireland" title="All-Ireland">All-Ireland</a> basis.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Greece">Greece</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Greece"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Despite having an ancient tradition with well-documented history, all racetracks in Greece have ceased operation due to the <a href="/wiki/Austerity_measures" class="mw-redirect" title="Austerity measures">Greek government-debt crisis</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>57<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Hungary">Hungary</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Hungary"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Hungary has a long-standing horse racing tradition. The first horse racing in Pest was noted on June 6, 1827.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2014)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Although racing in Hungary is neither as popular nor as prestigious as it is in Western Europe, the country is notable for producing some fine international racehorses. Foremost of these is <a href="/wiki/Kincsem" title="Kincsem">Kincsem</a>, foaled in 1874 and the most successful Thoroughbred racehorse ever, having won 54 races in 54 starts. The country also produced <a href="/wiki/Overdose_(horse)" title="Overdose (horse)">Overdose</a>, a horse who won his first 12 races, including <a href="/wiki/Group_race" class="mw-redirect" title="Group race">group races</a> in Germany and Italy, and finished fourth in the <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Stand_Stakes" class="mw-redirect" title="King&#39;s Stand Stakes">King\'s Stand Stakes</a> at <a href="/wiki/Royal_Ascot" class="mw-redirect" title="Royal Ascot">Royal Ascot</a>.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Ireland">Ireland</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Ireland"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Horse_racing_in_Ireland" title="Horse racing in Ireland">Horse racing in Ireland</a></div>\n<p>Ireland has a rich history of horse racing; <a href="/wiki/Point_to_point_(steeplechase)" class="mw-redirect" title="Point to point (steeplechase)">point to pointing</a> originated there, and even today, <a href="/wiki/National_Hunt_racing" title="National Hunt racing">jump racing</a> is more popular than racing on the flat. As a result, every year Irish horse racing fans travel in huge numbers to the highlight event of the National Hunt calendar, the <a href="/wiki/Cheltenham_Festival" title="Cheltenham Festival">Cheltenham Festival</a>, and in recent years Irish owned or bred horses have dominated the event.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2014)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Ireland has a thriving Thoroughbred breeding industry, stimulated by favorable tax treatment.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (February 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> The world\'s largest Thoroughbred stud farm, <a href="/wiki/Coolmore_Stud" title="Coolmore Stud">Coolmore Stud</a>, has its main site there (in addition to major operations in the U.S. and Australia).\n</p><p>In recent years,<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Chronological_items" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers"><span title="The time period mentioned near this tag is ambiguous. (February 2019)">when?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> various Irish bred and trained horses achieved victory in one or more of the <a href="/wiki/2000_Guineas" class="mw-redirect" title="2000 Guineas">British 2000 Guineas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Epsom_Derby" title="Epsom Derby">The Derby</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Prix_de_l%27Arc_de_Triomphe" title="Prix de l&#39;Arc de Triomphe">Prix de l\'Arc de Triomphe</a>, considered the three most prestigious races in Europe. In the six runnings of the Epsom Derby between 2008 and 2013, Irish horses filled 20 of the first 30 placings, winning the race 5 times.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (February 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Italy">Italy</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Italy"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_horse_races#Italy" title="List of horse races">List of horse races in Italy</a></div>\n<p>Historically, Italy has been one of the leading European horse-racing nations, albeit in some respects behind Great Britain, Ireland, and France in size and prestige. The late Italian horse breeder <a href="/wiki/Federico_Tesio" title="Federico Tesio">Federico Tesio</a> was particularly notable. In recent years, however, the sport in the country has suffered a major funding crisis, culminating in its 2014 expulsion from the European <a href="/wiki/Pattern_races" class="mw-redirect" title="Pattern races">Pattern</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-RP140416_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RP140416-58"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>58<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Netherlands">Netherlands</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Netherlands"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link Hague</a> there is a grass course at <a href="/wiki/Duindigt" title="Duindigt">Duindigt</a>.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Poland">Poland</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Poland"><span>edit</span></a><span ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div class="mbox-image-div"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" The first regular horse racing was organized in 1841 on <a href="/wiki/Mokot%C3%B3w_Field" title="Mokot\xc3\xb3w Field">Mokot\xc3\xb3w Fields</a> in <a href="/wiki/Warsaw" title="Warsaw">Warsaw</a> by Towarzystwo Wy\xc5\x9bcig\xc3\xb3w Konnych i Wystawy Zwierz\xc4\x85t Gospodarskich w Kr\xc3\xb3lestwie Polskim (in English, the Society of Horse Racing in Congress Poland). The main racetrack in Poland is Warsaw\'s S\xc5\x82u\xc5\xbcewiec Racecourse. The industry was severely limited during the <a href="/wiki/Communist" class="mw-redirect" title="Communist">Communist</a> era, when gambling, the major source of funding, was made illegal.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Sweden">Sweden</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Sweden"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Harness_racing_in_Sweden" title="Harness racing in Sweden">Harness racing in Sweden</a></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236091366"><table class="box-Unreferenced_section plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div class="mbox-image-div"><span typeof="mw:File"><a decoding="async" width="50" height="39" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, in Sweden, with significant amounts of money wagered annually.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Oceania">Oceania</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Oceania"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Australia">Australia</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Australia"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Thoroughbred_racing_in_Australia" title="Thoroughbred racing in Australia">Thoroughbred racing in Australia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Harness_racing_in_Australia" title="Harness racing in Australia">Harness racing in Australia</a></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Tambo_valley_races_2006_edit.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d2/Tambo_valley_races_2006_edit.jpg/220px-Tambo_valley_races_2006_edit.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d2/Tambo_valley_races_2006_edit.jpg/330px-Tambo_valley_races_2006_edit.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d2/Tambo_valley_races_2006_edit.jpg/440px-Tambo_valley_races_2006_edit.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1600" data-file-height="1067" /></a><figcaption><a href="/wiki/Tambo_Valley" class="mw-redirect" title="Tambo Valley">Tambo Valley</a> Picnic Races, Victoria, Australia 2006</figcaption></figure>\n<p>Horse racing in Australia was founded during the early years of settlement and the industry has grown to be among the top three leading Thoroughbred racing nations of the world.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>59<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The world-famous <a href="/wiki/Melbourne_Cup" title="Melbourne Cup">Melbourne Cup</a>, the <i>race that stops a nation</i>, has recently attracted many international entries. In country racing, records indicate that Goulburn commenced racing in 1834.<sup id="cite_ref-Barrie_2_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Barrie_2-60"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>60<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Australia\'s first country racing club was established at Wallabadah in 1852 and the Wallabadah Cup is still held on New Year\'s Day (the current racecourse was built in 1898).<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>61<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>In Australia, the most famous racehorse was <a href="/wiki/Phar_Lap" title="Phar Lap">Phar Lap</a> (bred in New Zealand), who raced from 1928 to 1932. Phar Lap carried <span class="nowrap">9 st 12 lb (62.5 kg)</span> to win the 1930 Melbourne Cup. Australian <a href="/wiki/Steeplechase_(horse_racing)" title="Steeplechase (horse racing)">steeplechaser</a> <a href="/wiki/Crisp_(horse)" title="Crisp (horse)">Crisp</a> is remembered for his battle with Irish champion <a href="/wiki/Red_Rum" title="Red Rum">Red Rum</a> in the 1973 <a href="/wiki/Grand_National" title="Grand National">Grand National</a>. In 2003\xe2\x80\x932005 the mare <a href="/wiki/Makybe_Diva" title="Makybe Diva">Makybe Diva</a> (bred in Great Britain) became the only racehorse to ever win the <a href="/wiki/Melbourne_Cup" title="Melbourne Cup">Melbourne Cup</a> three times, let alone in consecutive years. Still more recently, another mare, <a href="/wiki/Winx_(horse)" title="Winx (horse)">Winx</a>. won the prestigious <a href="/wiki/W._S._Cox_Plate" title="W. S. Cox Plate">Cox Plate</a> four straight times, and set a modern-era world record for most consecutive race wins by a Thoroughbred, winning the last 33 races of her career. In <a href="/wiki/Harness_racing" title="Harness racing">harness racing</a>, Cane Smoke had 120 wins, including 34 in a single season, <a href="/wiki/Paleface_Adios" title="Paleface Adios">Paleface Adios</a> became a household name during the 1970s, while <a href="/wiki/Cardigan_Bay_(horse)" title="Cardigan Bay (horse)">Cardigan Bay</a>, a pacing horse from New Zealand, enjoyed great success at the highest levels of American harness racing in the 1960s. More recently, <a href="/wiki/Blacks_A_Fake" title="Blacks A Fake">Blacks A Fake</a> has won four <a href="/wiki/Inter_Dominion" title="Inter Dominion">Inter Dominion</a> Championships, making him the only horse to complete this feat in Australasia\'s premier harness race.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>62<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Competitive endurance riding commenced in Australia in 1966, when the Tom Quilty Gold Cup was first held in the Hawkesbury district, near Sydney. The Quilty Cup is considered the National endurance ride and there are now over 100 endurance events contested across Australia, ranging in distances from 80&#160;km to 400 km.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>63<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The world\'s longest endurance ride is the <a href="/wiki/Shahzada_(horse_race)" title="Shahzada (horse race)">Shahzada</a> 400&#160;km Memorial Test which is conducted over five days traveling 80 kilometers a day at St Albans on the <a href="/wiki/Hawkesbury_River" title="Hawkesbury River">Hawkesbury River</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_South_Wales" title="New South Wales">New South Wales</a>. In all endurance events, there are rigorous vet checks, conducted before, during and after the competition, in which the horses\' welfare is of the utmost concern.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>64<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="New_Zealand">New Zealand</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: New Zealand"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Thoroughbred_racing_in_New_Zealand" title="Thoroughbred racing in New Zealand">Thoroughbred racing in New Zealand</a> and <a href="/wiki/Harness_racing_in_New_Zealand" title="Harness racing in New Zealand">Harness racing in New Zealand</a></div>\n<p>Racing is a long-established sport in New Zealand, stretching back to colonial times.\n</p><p>Horse racing is a significant part of the New Zealand economy which in 2004 generated 1.3% of the GDP. The indirect impact of expenditures on racing was estimated to have generated more than $1.4&#160;billion in economic activity in 2004 and created 18,300 full-time equivalent jobs. More than 40,000 people were involved in some capacity in the New Zealand racing industry in 2004. In 2004, more than one million people attended race meetings in New Zealand.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>65<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> There are 69 Thoroughbred and 51 harness clubs licensed in New Zealand. Racecourses are situated in 59 locations throughout New Zealand.\n</p><p>The bloodstock industry is important to New Zealand, with the export sale of horses \xe2\x80\x93 mainly to Australia and Asia \xe2\x80\x93 generating more than $120&#160;million a year. During the 2008\xe2\x80\x9309 racing season 19 New Zealand bred horses won 22 Group One races around the world.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>66<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Notable thoroughbred racehorses from New Zealand include <a href="/wiki/Carbine_(horse)" title="Carbine (horse)">Carbine</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nightmarch" title="Nightmarch">Nightmarch</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sunline" title="Sunline">Sunline</a>, <a href="/wiki/Desert_Gold_(horse)" title="Desert Gold (horse)">Desert Gold</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rising_Fast" title="Rising Fast">Rising Fast</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-de_Bourg_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-de_Bourg-67"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>67<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Digby_68-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Digby-68"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>68<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Phar_Lap" title="Phar Lap">Phar Lap</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tulloch_(horse)" title="Tulloch (horse)">Tulloch</a> were both bred in New Zealand but did not race there.\n</p><p>The most famous New Zealand standardbred horse is probably Cardigan Bay. <a href="/wiki/Stanley_Dancer" title="Stanley Dancer">Stanley Dancer</a> drove the New Zealand bred horse, Cardigan Bay to win $1&#160;million in stakes in 1968, the first harness horse to surpass that milestone in <a href="/wiki/American_history" class="mw-redirect" title="American history">American history</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>69<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Other horses of note include <a href="/wiki/Young_Quinn" title="Young Quinn">Young Quinn</a>, <a href="/wiki/Christian_Cullen_(horse)" title="Christian Cullen (horse)">Christian Cullen</a>, Lazarus and the trotter <a href="/wiki/Lyell_Creek" title="Lyell Creek">Lyell Creek</a>.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Africa">Africa</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Africa"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Mauritius">Mauritius</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Mauritius"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Maiden_Cup_2006,_Champ_de_Mars_Racecourse,_Port_Louis,_Mauritius_-_20060910.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Maiden_Cup_2006%2C_Champ_de_Mars_Racecourse%2C_Port_Louis%2C_Mauritius_-_20060910.jpg/220px-Maiden_Cup_2006%2C_Champ_de_Mars_Racecourse%2C_Port_Louis%2C_Mauritius_-_20060910.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Maiden_Cup_2006%2C_Champ_de_Mars_Racecourse%2C_Port_Louis%2C_Mauritius_-_20060910.jpg/330px-Maiden_Cup_2006%2C_Champ_de_Mars_Racecourse%2C_Port_Louis%2C_Mauritius_-_20060910.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Maiden_Cup_2006%2C_Champ_de_Mars_Racecourse%2C_Port_Louis%2C_Mauritius_-_20060910.jpg/440px-Maiden_Cup_2006%2C_Champ_de_Mars_Racecourse%2C_Port_Louis%2C_Mauritius_-_20060910.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2048" data-file-height="1536" /></a><figcaption>Maiden Cup 2006 - To The Line, winner of the race</figcaption></figure>\n<p>On 25 June 1812, the <a href="/wiki/Champ_de_Mars_Racecourse" title="Champ de Mars Racecourse">Champ de Mars Racecourse</a> was inaugurated by The <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauritius_Turf_Club&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Mauritius Turf Club (page does not exist)">Mauritius Turf Club</a> which was founded earlier in the same year by Colonel <a href="/wiki/Edward_A._Draper" class="mw-redirect" title="Edward A. Draper">Edward A. Draper</a>. The Champ de Mars is situated on a prestigious avenue in <a href="/wiki/Port_Louis" title="Port Louis">Port Louis</a>, the capital city and is the oldest racecourse in the <a href="/wiki/Southern_hemisphere" class="mw-redirect" title="Southern hemisphere">southern hemisphere</a>. The Mauritius Turf Club is the second oldest active turf club in the world.\n</p><p>Undeniably, racing is one of the most popular sports in <a href="/wiki/Mauritius" title="Mauritius">Mauritius</a> now attracting regular crowds of 20,000 people or more to the only racecourse of the island.\n</p><p>A high level of professionalism has been attained in the organization of races over the last decades preserving the unique electrifying ambiance prevailing on race days at the Champ de Mars.\n</p><p>Members of the <a href="/wiki/British_royal_family" title="British royal family">British royal family</a>, such as <a href="/wiki/Queen_Elizabeth_II" class="mw-redirect" title="Queen Elizabeth II">Queen Elizabeth II</a>, <a href="/wiki/Princess_Margaret" class="mw-redirect" title="Princess Margaret">Princess Margaret</a> or <a href="/wiki/Queen_Elizabeth_The_Queen_Mother" title="Queen Elizabeth The Queen Mother">Queen Elizabeth The Queen Mother</a> have attended or patronized races at the Champ de Mars numerous times.\n</p><p>Champ de Mars has four classic events a year such as the Duchess of York Cup, the Barb\xc3\xa9 Cup, the Maiden Cup, and the Duke of York Cup.\n</p><p>Most of the horses are imported from South Africa but some are also acquired from Australia, the United Kingdom and France.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>70<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>71<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>72<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>73<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>74<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>75<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>76<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>77<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="South_Africa">South Africa</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: South Africa"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Horse racing is a popular sport in South Africa that can be traced back to 1797. The first recorded race club meeting took place five years later in 1802.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>78<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The national horse racing body is known as the <a href="/wiki/National_Horseracing_Authority" title="National Horseracing Authority">National Horseracing Authority</a> and was founded in 1882. The premier event, which attracts 50,000 people to Durban, is the <a href="/wiki/Durban_July_Handicap" title="Durban July Handicap">Durban July Handicap</a>, which has been run since 1897 at <a href="/wiki/Greyville_Racecourse" title="Greyville Racecourse">Greyville Racecourse</a>. It is the largest and most prestigious event on the continent, with betting running into the hundreds of millions of Rands. Several July winners have gone on to win major international races, such as Colorado King, London News, and Ipi Tombe.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>79<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> However, the other notable major races are the Summer Cup, held at <a href="/wiki/Turffontein_Racecourse" title="Turffontein Racecourse">Turffontein Racecourse</a> in <a href="/wiki/Johannesburg" title="Johannesburg">Johannesburg</a>, and The Sun Met, which is held at <a href="/wiki/Kenilworth_Racecourse_Conservation_Area" title="Kenilworth Racecourse Conservation Area">Kenilworth race track</a> in <a href="/wiki/Cape_Town" title="Cape Town">Cape Town</a>.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Asia">Asia</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Asia"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="China">China</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: China"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Horse_racing_held_at_Third_Month_Fair_in_Yunnan.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Horse_racing_held_at_Third_Month_Fair_in_Yunnan.jpg/220px-Horse_racing_held_at_Third_Month_Fair_in_Yunnan.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="144" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Horse_racing_held_at_Third_Month_Fair_in_Yunnan.jpg/330px-Horse_racing_held_at_Third_Month_Fair_in_Yunnan.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Horse_racing_held_at_Third_Month_Fair_in_Yunnan.jpg/440px-Horse_racing_held_at_Third_Month_Fair_in_Yunnan.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1031" data-file-height="675" /></a><figcaption>Horse racing held at <a href="/wiki/Third_Month_Fair" title="Third Month Fair">Third Month Fair</a> in <a href="/wiki/Yunnan" title="Yunnan">Yunnan</a>, 2024</figcaption></figure>\n<p>Horse racing in one form or another has been a part of Chinese culture for millennia. Horse racing was a popular pastime for the aristocracy at least by the <a href="/wiki/Zhou_dynasty" title="Zhou dynasty">Zhou dynasty</a> \xe2\x80\x93 4th century B.C. General <a href="/wiki/Tian_Ji" title="Tian Ji">Tian Ji</a>\'s stratagem for a horse race remains perhaps the best-known story about horse racing in that period. In the 18th and 19th centuries, horse racing and equestrian sports in China was dominated by <a href="/wiki/Mongol" class="mw-redirect" title="Mongol">Mongol</a> influences.\n</p><p>Thoroughbred horse racing came to China with British settlements in the middle 1800s and most notably centered around the treaty ports, including the two major race courses in Shanghai, the <a href="/wiki/Shanghai_Race_Club" title="Shanghai Race Club">Shanghai Racecourse</a> and the International Recreation Grounds (in Kiang-wan), and the racecourses of <a href="/wiki/Tianjin" title="Tianjin">Tianjin</a>. The Kiang-wan racecourse was destroyed in the lead-up to the <a href="/wiki/Second_Sino-Japanese_War" title="Second Sino-Japanese War">Second Sino-Japanese War</a> and the Shanghai Race Club closed in 1954. The former Shanghai Racecourse is now People\'s Square and People\'s Park and the former club building was the <a href="/wiki/Shanghai_Art_Museum" class="mw-redirect" title="Shanghai Art Museum">Shanghai Art Museum</a>.\n</p><p>As Hong Kong and <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a> are <a href="/wiki/Special_Administrative_Regions" class="mw-redirect" title="Special Administrative Regions">Special Administrative Region</a>, they\'re allowed to exemption from ban of gambling on mainland China. (See below)\n</p><p>Horse racing was banned in the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China_(1912%E2%80%931949)" title="Republic of China (1912\xe2\x80\x931949)">Republic of China</a> from 1945, and the People\'s Republic of China maintained the ban after 1949, although allowances were made for ethnic minority peoples for whom horse sports are a cultural tradition. Speed horse racing (\xe9\x80\x9f\xe5\xba\xa6\xe8\xb5\x9b\xe9\xa9\xac) was an event in the <a href="/wiki/National_Games_of_China" title="National Games of China">National Games of China</a>, mainly introduced to cater to minority peoples, such as the <a href="/wiki/Mongols" title="Mongols">Mongols</a>. The racecourse was initially 5&#160;km, but from 2005 (the 10th National Games) was extended to 12&#160;km. The longer race led to deaths and injuries to participating horses in both 2005 and the 11th National Games in 2009. Also, with the entry into the sport of <a href="/wiki/Han_Chinese" title="Han Chinese">Han majority</a> provinces such as <a href="/wiki/Hubei" title="Hubei">Hubei</a>, which are better funded and used Western, rather than traditional, breeding and training techniques, meant that the original purpose of the event to foster traditional horse racing for groups like the Mongols was at risk of being usurped. At the 2009 National Games, Hubei won both the gold and silver medals, with <a href="/wiki/Inner_Mongolia" title="Inner Mongolia">Inner Mongolia</a> winning bronze. As a result of these factors, the event was abolished for the 12th National Games in 2013.\n</p><p>Club horse racing reappeared on a small scale in the 1990s. In 2008, the China Speed Horse Race Open in <a href="/wiki/Wuhan" title="Wuhan">Wuhan</a> was organized as the qualification round for the speed horse race event at the National Games the next year, but was also seen by commentators as a step towards legalizing both horse racing and gambling on the races.<sup id="cite_ref-Reuters_80-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Reuters-80"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>80<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The Wuhan Racecourse was the only racecourse that organized races in China.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>81<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In 2014, the Wuhan Jockey Club organized more than 80 races. Almost all Chinese trainers and jockeys stabled in Wuhan. However, with the demise of the event at the National Games and the government not relenting from the ban on commercial racing, various racecourses built in recent years are all in a state of disuse: The Nanjing Racecourse, which previously hosted National Games equestrian events, is now used as a car park;<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>82<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Beijing_Jockey_Club" title="Beijing Jockey Club">Beijing Jockey Club</a> was shut down in 2008. The racecourse in <a href="/wiki/Inner_Mongolia" title="Inner Mongolia">Inner Mongolia</a> has not been active since 2012.\n</p><p>Horse racing eventually returned to mainland China on the year 2014 as the one-day, five-card event for foreign horses, trainers and jockeys.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>83<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Standardized horse racing events have gradually emerged in China.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>84<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Hong_Kong">Hong Kong</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Hong Kong"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Hongkongjockeyclub.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Hongkongjockeyclub.jpg/220px-Hongkongjockeyclub.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="134" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Hongkongjockeyclub.jpg/330px-Hongkongjockeyclub.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Hongkongjockeyclub.jpg/440px-Hongkongjockeyclub.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1784" data-file-height="1084" /></a><figcaption><a href="/wiki/Happy_Valley_Racecourse" title="Happy Valley Racecourse">Happy Valley Racecourse</a> in Hong Kong at night</figcaption></figure>\n<p>The British tradition of horse racing left its mark with the creation of one of the most important entertainment and gambling institutions in Hong Kong. Established as the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Hong_Kong_Jockey_Club" class="mw-redirect" title="Royal Hong Kong Jockey Club">Royal Hong Kong Jockey Club</a> in 1884, the non-profit organization conducts nearly 700 races every season at the two race tracks: in <a href="/wiki/Happy_Valley_Racecourse" title="Happy Valley Racecourse">Happy Valley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sha_Tin_Racecourse" title="Sha Tin Racecourse">Sha Tin</a>.\n</p><p>All horses are imported since there is no breeding operation.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (February 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> The sport annually draws millions of dollars of tax revenue. Off-track betting is available from overseas bookmakers.\n</p><p>In the 1920s, the Hong Kong Jockey Club had race meetings for visitors already. Visitors were divided into public and member. The charges for these two types of visitors are different.\n</p><p>The charge for admission to the Public Enclosure is $1 per day for all while soldiers and sailors can enjoy half price. On the other hand, members are required to show their badges to obtain admission to the Members\' Enclosure. And also the charge for admission to the Members\' Enclosure is $2 per day.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>85<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> By comparing the lowest wage in 1929, we observe that the lowest wage is around $12 ( $0.4 per day) which has a large distance for the requirement enclosure.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>86<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Therefore, we can observe that the race meetings are mainly opened for upper class mostly while grass-root has a lower chance to touch horse racing activity.\n</p><p>Nowadays, the Hong Kong Jockey Club is a cornerstone of modern Hong Kong. It donates all its profits to the Hong Kong government, charities and public institutions. It is the territory\'s largest taxpayer, contributing 11% of the government\'s revenues in 2000. In economic terms, the Hong Kong Jockey Club is an old-fashioned government-protected monopoly; all other forms of gambling are illegal in this industry.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>87<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading5"><h5 id="Hong_Kong\xe2\x80\x94Sweepstakes"><span id="Hong_Kong.E2.80.94Sweepstakes"></span>Hong Kong\xe2\x80\x94Sweepstakes</h5><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Hong Kong\xe2\x80\x94Sweepstakes"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Sweepstakes were introduced in Hong Kong during the 1920s. There are three types of sweepstakes which are the Special Cash Sweeps, the Last Race Sweep and the Ordinary Cash Sweeps. Special Cash Sweeps were at first drawn twice a year, and increased to three times a year later given its popularity. It carried the highest prize money amongst three types of sweepstakes. The Last Race Sweep commanded higher prize money then Ordinary Cash Sweeps, which were drawn for almost every race and therefore carried the lowest prize money.<sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_88-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-88"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>88<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Sweepstakes could be purchased either at sweepstakes stations or from sweepstakes vendors throughout Hong Kong. With different numbers print on each sweepstake, one sweepstake is drawn and assigned, for each horse participating in the race, and the sweepstake attached to the winning horse would win the first prize. Likewise, the number of the first runner-up and second runner-up would win the second and third prize, respectively, with the rest winning consolation prizes. With the introduction of new bet types in horse racing and the launch of the Mark Six lottery in the 1970s, the club finally stopped selling sweepstakes in 1977.<sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_88-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-88"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>88<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Macau">Macau</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Macau"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Jockey Club of Macau was established for harness racing. It started to conduct horse races in 1989.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>89<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="India">India</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: India"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Horse_racing_in_India" title="Horse racing in India">Horse racing in India</a></div><p>India\'s first racecourse was set up in Madras in 1777, <a href="/wiki/Guindy_Race_Course" title="Guindy Race Course">Guindy race course</a>. Today India has nine racetracks operated by seven racing authorities.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (February 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p><div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Japan">Japan</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Japan"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Horse_racing_in_Japan" title="Horse racing in Japan">Horse racing in Japan</a></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Nakayama_Racecourse01.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Nakayama_Racecourse01.jpg/220px-Nakayama_Racecourse01.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="85" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Nakayama_Racecourse01.jpg/330px-Nakayama_Racecourse01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Nakayama_Racecourse01.jpg/440px-Nakayama_Racecourse01.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1213" data-file-height="469" /></a><figcaption><a href="/wiki/Nakayama_Racecourse" title="Nakayama Racecourse">Nakayama Racecourse</a> in Funabashi, Japan</figcaption></figure>\n<p>Japan has two governing bodies that control its horseracing \xe2\x80\x93 the <a href="/wiki/Japan_Racing_Association" title="Japan Racing Association">Japan Racing Association</a> (JRA), and <a href="/wiki/National_Association_of_Racing" title="National Association of Racing">National Association of Racing</a> (NAR). Between them they conduct more than 21,000 horse races a year. The JRA is responsible for horseracing events at ten major racecourses in metropolitan areas, while the NAR is responsible for various local horseracing events throughout Japan. Racing in Japan is mainly <a href="/wiki/Flat_racing" class="mw-redirect" title="Flat racing">flat racing</a>, but Japan also has <a href="/wiki/Jump_racing" class="mw-redirect" title="Jump racing">jump racing</a> and a sled-pulling race known as <a href="/wiki/Ban%27ei" title="Ban&#39;ei">Ban\'ei</a> (also called Draft Racing).\n</p><p>Japan\'s top stakes races are run in the spring, autumn, and winter. These include the country\'s most prominent race \xe2\x80\x93 the Grade 1 <a href="/wiki/Japan_Cup" title="Japan Cup">Japan Cup</a>, a 2,400 m (about 1\xc2\xbd mile) invitational turf race run every November at <a href="/wiki/Tokyo_Racecourse" title="Tokyo Racecourse">Tokyo Racecourse</a> for a purse of \xc2\xa5476&#160; million (about US$5.6&#160;million), one of the richest turf races in the world. Other noted stakes races include the <a href="/wiki/February_Stakes" title="February Stakes">February Stakes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Japanese_Derby" class="mw-redirect" title="Japanese Derby">Japanese Derby</a>, <a href="/wiki/Takamatsunomiya_Kinen" title="Takamatsunomiya Kinen">Takamatsunomiya Kinen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yasuda_Kinen" title="Yasuda Kinen">Yasuda Kinen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Takarazuka_Kinen" title="Takarazuka Kinen">Takarazuka Kinen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arima_Kinen" title="Arima Kinen">Arima Kinen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Satsuki_Sho" class="mw-redirect" title="Satsuki Sho">Satsuki Sho</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kikka_Sho" class="mw-redirect" title="Kikka Sho">Kikka Sho</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Tenno_Sho" title="Tenno Sho">Tenno Sho</a> races run in the spring and fall. Japan\'s top jump race is the <a href="/wiki/Nakayama_Grand_Jump" title="Nakayama Grand Jump">Nakayama Grand Jump</a>, run every April at <a href="/wiki/Nakayama_Racecourse" title="Nakayama Racecourse">Nakayama Racecourse</a>.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Malaysia">Malaysia</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Malaysia"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>In <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a>, horse racing was introduced during the British colonial era and remains to the present day as a gambling activity. There are three race courses in Peninsular Malaysia, namely <a href="/wiki/Penang_Turf_Club" title="Penang Turf Club">Penang Turf Club</a>, Perak Turf Club, and <a href="/wiki/Selangor_Turf_Club" title="Selangor Turf Club">Selangor Turf Club</a>. Within and only within the turf clubs, betting on horse racing is a legal form of gambling. Racing in Peninsular Malaysia and Singapore is conducted and governed under the Rules of the Malayan Racing Association and betting in Malaysia is operated and organized by Pan Malaysian Pools Sdn Bhd. In East Malaysia, races are governed independently by the Royal Sabah Turf Club<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>90<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> and the Sarawak Turf Club.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>91<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Mongolia">Mongolia</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Mongolia"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Mongolian horse racing takes place during the <a href="/wiki/Naadam" title="Naadam">Naadam</a> festival. Mongolia does not have Thoroughbred horse racing. Rather, it has its own Mongolian style of horse racing in which the horses run for at least a distance of 25 kilometers.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>92<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Pakistan">Pakistan</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Pakistan"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Horse races are held in Pakistan at four clubs. In Lahore at <a href="/wiki/Lahore_Race_Club" title="Lahore Race Club">Lahore Race Club</a>, Rawalpindi at Chakri, in Karachi at <a href="/wiki/Karachi_Race_Club" title="Karachi Race Club">Karachi Race Club</a>, and in Gujrat at Gujrat Race Club.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Philippines">Philippines</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Philippines"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Horseracing_in_the_Philippines" class="mw-redirect" title="Horseracing in the Philippines">Horseracing in the Philippines</a></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Horseracing_in_the_Philippines" class="mw-redirect" title="Horseracing in the Philippines">Horseracing in the Philippines</a> began in 1867. The history of Philippine horseracing has three divisions according to the breeds of horses used. They are the Philippine-pony era (1867\xe2\x80\x931898), the Arabian-horse era (1898\xe2\x80\x931930), and the Thoroughbred-era (1935\xe2\x80\x93present).<sup id="cite_ref-PRC_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PRC-93"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>93<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Singapore">Singapore</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Singapore"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236091366"><table class="box-Unreferenced_section plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div class="mbox-image-div"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="mw-file-description"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="39" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></span></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/Horse_racing" title="Special:EditPage/Horse racing">improve this Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span>  <span class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">January 2022</span>)</i></span><span class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<small><a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this message</a></small>)</i></span></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>Horse racing was introduced to Singapore by the British during the colonial era and remained one of the legal forms of gambling after independence. It remains a highly popular form of entertainment with the local Singaporean community to this day. Races are typically held on Friday evenings and Sundays at the <a href="/wiki/Singapore_Turf_Club" title="Singapore Turf Club">Singapore Turf Club</a> in <a href="/wiki/Kranji" title="Kranji">Kranji</a>. Horse racing has also left its mark in the naming of roads in Singapore such as Race Course Road in <a href="/wiki/Little_India,_Singapore" title="Little India, Singapore">Little India</a>, where horse racing was first held in Singapore, and Turf Club Road in <a href="/wiki/Bukit_Timah" title="Bukit Timah">Bukit Timah</a> where Singapore Turf Club used to be situated before moving to its current location in 1999.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (February 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="South_Korea">South Korea</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: South Korea"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Horse_racing_in_South_Korea" title="Horse racing in South Korea">Horse racing in South Korea</a></div>\n<p>Horse racing in South Korea dates back to May 1898, when a foreign language institute run by the government included a donkey race in its athletic rally. However, it wasn\'t until the 1920s that modern horse racing involving <a href="/wiki/Betting" class="mw-redirect" title="Betting">betting</a> developed. The nation\'s first authorised club, the Chosun Racing Club, was established in 1922 and a year later, the <a href="/wiki/Parimutuel_betting" title="Parimutuel betting">pari-mutuel betting system</a> was officially adopted for the first time.<sup id="cite_ref-ARFKorea_94-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ARFKorea-94"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>94<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Korean_War" title="Korean War">Korean War</a> disrupted the development of horse racing in the country, but after the <a href="/wiki/Seoul_Olympics" class="mw-redirect" title="Seoul Olympics">Seoul Olympics</a> in 1988, the Olympic Equestrian Park was converted into racing facilities named <a href="/wiki/Seoul_Race_Park" class="mw-redirect" title="Seoul Race Park">Seoul Race Park</a>, which helped the sport to develop again.<sup id="cite_ref-ARFKorea_94-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ARFKorea-94"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>94<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Turkey">Turkey</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Turkey"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Jockey_Club_of_Turkey" title="Jockey Club of Turkey">Jockey Club of Turkey</a></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236091366"><table class="box-Unreferenced_section plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div class="mbox-image-div"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="mw-file-description"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="39" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></span></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/Horse_racing" title="Special:EditPage/Horse racing">improve this section</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Referencing_for_beginners" title="Help:Referencing for beginners">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span>  <span class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">January 2022</span>)</i></span><span class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<small><a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this message</a></small>)</i></span></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>Horses have been an important role in Turks\' lives throughout history. After the modern Republic Of Turkey was established in 1923 by Mustafa Kemal Atat\xc3\xbcrk, the number of breeding and racing Arabian and thoroughbred racehorses accelerated rapidly, especially after the beginning of the 1930s. The Jockey Club of Turkey, founded in 1950, was the turning point of both the Turkish breeding and racing industries.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="United_Arab_Emirates">United Arab Emirates</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: United Arab Emirates"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The big race in the <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates" title="United Arab Emirates">UAE</a> is the <a href="/wiki/Dubai_World_Cup" title="Dubai World Cup">Dubai World Cup</a>, a race with a purse of US$12 million, which was the largest purse in the world until being surpassed by <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Cup" title="Saudi Cup">the Saudi Cup</a>, a race in Riyadh with a $20&#160; million purse that held its first edition in 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>95<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Other races include the <a href="/wiki/Dubai_Kahayla_Classic" title="Dubai Kahayla Classic">Dubai Kahayla Classic</a> with a purse of US$250,000.\n</p><p>The Meydan Racecourse in Dubai, reportedly the world\'s largest race track, opened on March 27, 2010, for the Dubai World Cup race. The race track complex contains two tracks with seating for 60,000, a hotel, restaurants, theater and a museum.\n</p><p>There is no parimutuel betting in the UAE as gambling is illegal.<sup id="cite_ref-Telovation_96-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Telovation-96"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>96<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="South_America">South America</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: South America"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Argentina">Argentina</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Argentina"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>In Argentina the sport is known as turf. Some of the most famous racers are <a href="/wiki/Irineo_Leguisamo" title="Irineo Leguisamo">Irineo Leguisamo</a>, Vilmar Sanguinetti, Marina Lezcano, Jorge Valdivieso, Pablo Falero and Jorge Ricardo. The most notable Argentine horse of recent decades is <a href="/wiki/Invasor_(horse)" title="Invasor (horse)">Invasor</a>, who won Uruguay\'s Triple Crown in 2005; won four U.S. Grade I races in 2006, including the <a href="/wiki/2006_Breeders%27_Cup_Classic" title="2006 Breeders&#39; Cup Classic">Breeders\' Cup Classic</a>, on his way to being named that country\'s <a href="/wiki/American_Horse_of_the_Year" title="American Horse of the Year">Horse of the Year</a>; and ended his racing career in 2007 with two more Grade I/Group One wins, including the Dubai World Cup.\n</p><p>Carlos Gardel\'s tango <a href="/wiki/Por_una_cabeza" class="mw-redirect" title="Por una cabeza">Por una cabeza</a> is about horse racing, a sport of which he was a known fan. Gardel was a good friend of <a href="/wiki/Irineo_Leguisamo" title="Irineo Leguisamo">Irineo Leguisamo</a>, who is the most recognized Uruguayan jockey, who raced numerous years in Argentine.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (February 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Betting">Betting</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Betting"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Betting_on_horse_racing" title="Betting on horse racing">Betting on horse racing</a></div>\n<p>At many horse races, there is a gambling station, where gamblers can <a href="/wiki/Betting_on_horse_racing" title="Betting on horse racing">stake money on a horse</a>. Gambling on horses is prohibited at some tracks; Springdale Race Course, home of the nationally renowned <a href="/wiki/Toronto-Dominion_Bank" title="Toronto-Dominion Bank">TD Bank</a> Carolina Cup and Colonial Cup Steeplechase in <a href="/wiki/Camden,_South_Carolina" title="Camden, South Carolina">Camden, South Carolina</a>, is known as one of the tracks where betting is illegal, due to a 1951 law. Where gambling is allowed, most tracks offer <a href="/wiki/Parimutuel_betting" title="Parimutuel betting">parimutuel betting</a> where gamblers\' money is pooled and shared proportionally among the winners once a deduction is made from the pool. In some countries, such as the UK, Ireland, and Australia, an alternative and more popular facility is provided by <a href="/wiki/Bookmaker" title="Bookmaker">bookmakers</a> who effectively <a href="/wiki/Market_maker" title="Market maker">make a market</a> in odds. This allows the gambler to \'lock in\' odds on a horse at a particular time (known as \'taking the price\' in the UK). <a href="/wiki/Parimutuel_betting" title="Parimutuel betting">Parimutuel</a> gambling on races also provides not only purse money to participants but considerable tax revenue, with over $100&#160;billion wagered annually in 53 countries.<sup id="cite_ref-NTRA_97-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NTRA-97"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>97<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Deaths_and_injuries">Deaths and injuries</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Horse_racing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Deaths and injuries"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Anna Waller, a member of the Department of Emergency Medicine at the University of North Carolina, co-authored a four-year-long study of jockey injuries and stated to <i><a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">The New York Times</a></i> that "For every 1,000 jockeys you have riding [for one year], over 600 will have medically treated injuries." She added that almost 20% of these were serious head or neck injuries. The study reported 6,545 injuries during the years 1993\xe2\x80\x931996.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>98<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>99<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> More than 100 jockeys were killed in the United States between 1950 and 1987.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>100<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Horses also face <a href="/wiki/Racehorse_injuries" title="Racehorse injuries">dangers</a> in racing. 1.5 horses die out of every 1,000 starts in the United States.<sup id="cite_ref-abc_101-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-abc-101"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>101<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The U.S. Jockey Club in New York estimates that about 600 horses died at racetracks in 2006. The Jockey Club in Hong Kong reported a far lower figure of 0.58 horses per 1,000 starts. There is speculation that drugs used in horse racing in the United States, which are banned elsewhere, are responsible for the higher death rate in the United States.<sup id="cite_ref-abc_101-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-abc-101"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>101<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>In the Canadian province of <a href="/wiki/Ontario" title="Ontario">Ontario</a>, a study of 1,709 racehorse deaths between 2003 and 2015 found that the majority of deaths were attributable to "damage during exercise to the horses\' <a href="/wiki/Skeletal_system_of_the_horse" title="Skeletal system of the horse">musculoskeletal system</a>", including fractures, dislocations, and tendon ruptures.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>102<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Mortality rates were eight times higher for <a href="/wiki/Thoroughbred" title="Thoroughbred">thoroughbreds</a> than <a href="/wiki/Standardbred" title="Standardbred">standardbreds</a>, and highest amongst young horses. The study also found that the incidence of off-track deaths was twice as high for thoroughbreds.\n</p><p>In the United Kingdom, 186 horses were killed as a direct result of racing in 2019. Of these 145 died in National Hunt (jump) racing and 41 in flat racing.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>103<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> A report published in 2005 estimated that "around 375 horses who are entered into races each season die from their injuries, or they are killed because they are considered of no further commercial value, even though they are young enough to continue racing." It added, "Reasons for horses being destroyed include broken legs, back, neck and pelvis; fatal spinal injuries, exhaustion, heart attack, and burst blood vessels in the lungs."<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>104<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="See_also">See
